It depends on your personal needs. If you just want to take a look at Wanlu Lake, this boat ride is available. One lap is enough, but the disadvantage is that the engine is a bit noisy.

The room is old, peeling in many places, and the wooden edges are warped. The hotel swimming pool layer has a strong musty smell and heavy moisture. The outdoor swimming pool is quite big and fun, but there are a lot of mosaics found on the side of the swimming pool. They fell in the swimming pool, so be careful to cut your feet.
Environment: The main purpose of raising children is to play in the water. I came here for the swimming pool. The balcony view is very nice. Watching the stars at night is very healing. But what is strange is that there are no lights in the hotel yard at night. It is completely dark. I have not encountered it yet. This situationâ€¦
Service: I have to complain about the service. There are two bathrobes in one room. I forgot whether I have to pay 15 or 30 for each. The outdoor swimming pool closed at 7 o'clock, the water in the indoor swimming pool was very cold, and the power went out three times in half an hour of swimming. I was really drunk...
We met a guest staying in the same hotel at the swimming pool, and the reservation was 200 yuan cheaper than the one we booked with Ctrip.
